endHorizontalPosition = 2;\n        var endVerticalPosition = 2\n        var startClass = $('.start-location');\n        var endClass = $('.end-location');\n        var startStyle = 'position: fixed;z-index: inherit;width: inherit;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;background-color:inherit;border:inherit;';\n        var endStyle = 'position: fixed;z-index: inherit;width: inherit;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;background-color:inherit;border:inherit;';\n\n        if(animationType!= 1)\n        {\n            endStyle += 'transition: all ' + animationDuration + 's ease 0s;';\n        }\n\n        switch(endHorizontalPosition)\n        {\n            case 0:\n                startStyle += 'left:-' + $(obj).outerWidth() +'px;';\n                endStyle += case 2:\n                startStyle += 'right:-' + $(obj).outerWidth() + 'px;';\n                endStyle += 'right:0px;';\n                break;\n        }\n\n        //  Vertical animation is only used with central horizontal alignment\n        switch(endVerticalPosition)\n        {\n            case 0:\n                if(endHorizontalPosition==1)\n                {\n endStyle += 'top:0px;';\n                break;\n            case 1:\n                startStyle += 'top:44%';\n                endStyle += 'top:44%';\n                break;\n            case 2:\n                if(endHorizontalPosition==1)\n                {\n                     startStyle += 'bottom: -' + $(obj).outerHeight() + 'px;';\n                }\n                else\n {\n            $('#' + 'NavTop_EmailSubscriptionsPopup1_DivEndLocationClass').append('<style type=\"text/css\">.email-subscription-popup .end-location{' + endStyle + '}.email-subscription-popup
